- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls

# Firefox CSS Style Resolution to Layout Paint Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the style change notification, the frame style recomputation, the dirty-frame reflow scheduling, the display list construction, and the WebRender layer update.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

103-assistanttext-
The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here is a summary of the CSS style change → layout → paint chain I traced:

## The Chain

### 1. Style Change Notification
**`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** — `RestyleManager::PostRestyleEvent`

When CSS changes (inline style, class, attribute, etc.), `PostRestyleEvent()` calls `Servo_NoteExplicitHints()` into the Servo engine to mark the element dirty and set the document's "restyle root."

### 2. Style Traversal / Frame Style Recomputation
**`layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp`** — `ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument`  
**`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** — `RestyleManager::ProcessPostTraversal`

On the next flush, `RestyleManager::ProcessPendingRestyles()` calls `ServoStyleSet::StyleDocument()` which invokes `Servo_TraverseSubtree()` (parallel Servo style computation). The post-traversal calls `Servo_TakeChangeHint()` per frame to collect `nsChangeHint` entries into an `nsStyleChangeList`.

### 3. Dirty-Frame Reflow Scheduling
**`layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`** — `RestyleManager::ProcessRestyledFrames`, `StyleChangeReflow`  
**`layout/base/PresShell.cpp`** — `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow`

`ProcessRestyledFrames()` iterates change hints. Reflow hints go through `StyleChangeReflow()` → `PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow()` which marks frames with `NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY` and adds them to `mDirtyRoots`.

### 4. Reflow Execution
**`layout/base/PresShell.cpp`** — `PresShell::ProcessReflowCommands`

`DoFlushLayout()` → `ProcessReflowCommands()` pops dirty roots from `mDirtyRoots` and calls `DoReflow()` on each.

### 5. Display List Construction
**`layout/base/nsLayoutUtils.cpp`** — `nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame`  
**`layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp`** — `nsDisplayList::PaintRoot`

`PaintFrame()` creates an `nsDisplayListBuilder`
